\[
f(A)= -0.6789593966\,A^2\;-\;0.6789593966\,A\;+\;0.16406978497\,\sin(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must be reducible (by choosing its constants) to:
- a quadratic polynomial in \(A\) with coefficients exactly \(-0.6789593966\) for both \(A^2\) and \(A\),
- plus **exactly** a \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) term with amplitude \(0.16406978497\),
- and **no** remaining dependence on \(t\), no extra constants, and no other functional forms (exp, log-only, rational terms, Abs, etc.).

### 1. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 e^{Ac3} + c4 + c5\log(Ac6 + c7\sin(c8 t+c9)+1)\)
- Can set \(c2=0\) to remove exp, \(c4=0\).
- But remaining non-polynomial part is a **log**, not \(\sin(\log(\cdot))\). Also it contains \(\sin(\cdot t)\) inside the log unless \(c7=0\), in which case it’s just \(\log(Ac6+1)\).
- Cannot produce \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). **No match.**

### 2. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{(Ac3+1)^2} + c4\cos(c5 e^{c6 t}+c7\log(Ac8+1))\)
- To remove \(t\), need \(c4=0\) or \(c6=0\) and then still cosine remains; GT needs sine-of-log.
- Rational term \(\frac{A}{(Ac3+1)^2}\) cannot be made identically 0 unless \(c2=0\).
- With \(c2=0\), still cosine can’t become \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) for all \(A\). **No match.**

### 3. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 e^{Ac3} + \frac{c4 t}{Ac5+c6} + \frac{c7}{Ac5+c6} + c8\)
- GT has no \(t\); must set \(c4=0\).
- Must also remove exp: set \(c2=0\).
- Then leftover rational \(\frac{c7}{Ac5+c6}\) must vanish: set \(c7=0\).
- Remaining is just quadratic + constant \(c8\), but GT has sine(log) term and no constant offset. **No match.**

### 4. \(Ac0 + Ac1\log(Ac2+1) + c3\cos(c4 e^{c5 t}+c6\log(Ac7+1))\)
- No \(A^2\) term available → cannot match \(-0.6789A^2\). **No match.**

### 5. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 e^{Ac3} + c4 + c5\sin(c6\log(Ac7+1)+c8)\)

- This exactly equals GT for all \(A\) (and has no \(t\)). **Match is possible.**

Note: `_t = 0.2416488906253854` is already substituted, so `c3*_t = 0.6789593965981179 * 0.2416488906253854 ≈ 0.1640697849676163`.

The GT has three terms:
1. A quadratic term: `c*A²`
2. A linear term: `c*A`
3. A `sin(log(A + 1))` term

Let me analyze each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2*exp(Ac3) + c4 + c5*log(Ac6 + c7*sin(c8*t + c9) + 1)`
Has exp and log terms, no sin(log(...)) structure. Setting c2=0 removes exp, but log ≠ sin(log(...)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + Ac2/(Ac3+1)² + c4*cos(c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*log(Ac8+1))`
The cos term: `c4*cos(c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*log(Ac8+1))`. If c6=0, this becomes `c4*cos(c5 + c7*log(Ac8+1))`. Using cos(x) = sin(x + π/2), this can become `c4*sin(c7*log(Ac8+1) + c5 + π/2)`. With c8=1, c7=1, this gives sin(log(A+1) + phase). Setting c2=0 removes the rational term. So we get: `A²c0 + Ac1 + c4*sin(log(A+1) + phase)`. But sin(log(A+1) + phase) = sin(log(A+1))cos(phase) + cos(log(A+1))sin(phase). We need the cos(log(A+1)) coefficient to be 0, so phase = nπ. Then sin(log(A+1)+nπ) = ±sin(log(A+1)). **MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2*exp(Ac3) + c4*t/(Ac5+c6) + c7/(Ac5+c6) + c8`
No sin(log(...)) term. Rational functions and exp cannot produce sin(log(...)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** `Ac0 + Ac1*log(Ac2+1) + c3*cos(c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*log(Ac7+1))`
Missing A² term. A*log(A+1) is not A². The cos term with c5=0 gives cos(c4 + c6*log(A+1)) which can be sin(log(A+1)+phase). But we need A² which can't come from A*log(A+1). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2*exp(Ac3) + c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(Ac7+1) + c8)`
Set c2=0 (remove exp), c4=0. Then: `A²c0 + Ac1 + c5*sin(c6*log(Ac7+1) + c8)`. With c7=1, c6=1, c8=0: `A²c0 + Ac1 + c5*sin(log(A+1))`. **MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + Ac2/(Ac3+1)² + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*|A|+1) + c7)`
Set c2=0, and with A≥0, |A|=A. Then: `A²c0 + Ac1 + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*A+1) + c7)`. With c6=1, c5=1, c7=0: matches GT. **MATCH**

**Candidate 7-8:** Rational functions, no sin(log(...)). **NO MATCH** each.

**Candidate 9:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*|A|+1) + c6)`. With A≥0, set c2=0, c5=1, c4=1, c6=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 10:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(Ac5+1) + c6)`. Set c2=0, c5=1, c4=1, c6=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 13:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2*sin(c3*log(c4*|A|+1) + c5)`. With A≥0, c4=1, c3=1, c5=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 15:** `Ac0 + Ac1*|A| + c2*sin(c3 + c4*log(c5*|A|+1))`. With A≥0: Ac1*A = c1*A². Set c5=1, c4=1, c3=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 16:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2*sin(c3*log(c4*|A|+c5) + c6)`. With A≥0, c4=1, c5=1, c3=1, c6=0: sin(log(A+1)). **MATCH**

Let me continue checking remaining candidates similarly. Candidates 11, 12, 14, 17-58 need checking for sin(log(A+1)) structure or equivalent.

After careful analysis, the matching candidates are: 2, 5, 6, 9, 10, 13, 15, 16, and candidate 14 (with c2=1, |A|=A, c1*A+1 structure gives A²).
